import torch
import torch.nn as nn
import math
from torch.utils.cpp_extension import load_inline

CUDA_SOURCE = r"""
#include <torch/extension.h>
#include <cuda_runtime.h>
#include <math.h>

__global__ void preprocess_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ pair_repr,
    const float* __restrict__ ln_weight,
    const float* __restrict__ ln_bias,
    const float* __restrict__ W_query,
    const float* __restrict__ W_key,
    const float* __restrict__ W_value,
    const float* __restrict__ W_gate,
    const float* __restrict__ b_gate,
    const float* __restrict__ W_bias,
    float* __restrict__ q,
    float* __restrict__ k,
    float* __restrict__ v,
    float* __restrict__ gate,
    float* __restrict__ bias,
    int B, int N, int D, int h, int d
) {
    int pos = blockIdx.x;
    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    
    extern __shared__ float shared_mem[];
    float* x_shared = shared_mem;
    float* reduce_buf = shared_mem + 128;
    
    if (tid < D) {
        x_shared[tid] = pair_repr[pos * D + tid];
    }
    __syncthreads();
    
    if (tid < D) {
        reduce_buf[tid] = x_shared[tid];
    } else {
        reduce_buf[tid] = 0.0f;
    }
    __syncthreads();
    
    for (int stride = blockDim.x / 2; stride > 0; stride /= 2) {
        if (tid < stride) {
            reduce_buf[tid] += reduce_buf[tid + stride];
        }
        __syncthreads();
    }
    float mean = reduce_buf[0] / D;
    
    if (tid < D) {
        float diff = x_shared[tid] - mean;
        reduce_buf[tid] = diff * diff;
    } else {
        reduce_buf[tid] = 0.0f;
    }
    __syncthreads();
    
    for (int stride = blockDim.x / 2; stride > 0; stride /= 2) {
        if (tid < stride) {
            reduce_buf[tid] += reduce_buf[tid + stride];
        }
        __syncthreads();
    }
    float var = reduce_buf[0] / D;
    
    if (tid < D) {
        x_shared[tid] = (x_shared[tid] - mean) * rsqrtf(var + 1e-5f) * ln_weight[tid] + ln_bias[tid];
    }
    __syncthreads();
    
    int b = pos / (N * N);
    int rem = pos % (N * N);
    int i = rem / N;
    int j = rem % N;
    int r = b * N + i;
    
    for (int out_c = tid; out_c < D; out_c += blockDim.x) {
        float val = 0.0f;
        for (int c = 0; c < D; c++) {
            val += W_query[out_c * D + c] * x_shared[c];
        }
        int head = out_c / d;
        int dd = out_c % d;
        q[((r * h + head) * N + j) * d + dd] = val;
    }
    
    for (int out_c = tid; out_c < D; out_c += blockDim.x) {
        float val = 0.0f;
        for (int c = 0; c < D; c++) {
            val += W_key[out_c * D + c] * x_shared[c];
        }
        int head = out_c / d;
        int dd = out_c % d;
        k[((r * h + head) * N + j) * d + dd] = val;
    }
    
    for (int out_c = tid; out_c < D; out_c += blockDim.x) {
        float val = 0.0f;
        for (int c = 0; c < D; c++) {
            val += W_value[out_c * D + c] * x_shared[c];
        }
        int head = out_c / d;
        int dd = out_c % d;
        v[((r * h + head) * N + j) * d + dd] = val;
    }
    
    for (int out_c = tid; out_c < D; out_c += blockDim.x) {
        float val = b_gate[out_c];
        for (int c = 0; c < D; c++) {
            val += W_gate[out_c * D + c] * x_shared[c];
        }
        gate[pos * D + out_c] = 1.0f / (1.0f + expf(-val));
    }
    
    for (int out_c = tid; out_c < h; out_c += blockDim.x) {
        float val = 0.0f;
        for (int c = 0; c < D; c++) {
            val += W_bias[out_c * D + c] * x_shared[c];
        }
        bias[((b * h + out_c) * N + i) * N + j] = val;
    }
}

__global__ void attention_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ q,
    const float* __restrict__ k,
    const float* __restrict__ v,
    const float* __restrict__ bias,
    const float* __restrict__ pair_mask,
    float* __restrict__ scratch,
    int B, int N, int D, int h, int d
) {
    int b = blockIdx.x / (N * h);
    int rem = blockIdx.x % (N * h);
    int i = rem / h;
    int head = rem % h;
    int r = b * N + i;
    int query = threadIdx.x;
    
    if (query >= N) return;
    
    extern __shared__ float shared_mem2[];
    float* K_shared = shared_mem2;
    float* V_shared = shared_mem2 + N * d;
    
    for (int l = query; l < N * d; l += blockDim.x) {
        K_shared[l] = k[((r * h + head) * N) * d + l];
        V_shared[l] = v[((r * h + head) * N) * d + l];
    }
    __syncthreads();
    
    float q_local[64];
    for (int dd = 0; dd < d; dd++) {
        q_local[dd] = q[((r * h + head) * N + query) * d + dd];
    }
    
    float scores[64];
    float max_score = -1e9f;
    
    for (int key = 0; key < N; key++) {
        float dot = 0.0f;
        for (int dd = 0; dd < d; dd++) {
            dot += q_local[dd] * K_shared[key * d + dd];
        }
        float score = dot / sqrtf((float)d);
        score += bias[((b * h + head) * N + query) * N + key];
        if (pair_mask[(b * N + query) * N + key] == 0.0f) {
            score = -1e9f;
        }
        scores[key] = score;
        if (score > max_score) max_score = score;
    }
    
    float sum_exp = 0.0f;
    for (int key = 0; key < N; key++) {
        scores[key] = expf(scores[key] - max_score);
        sum_exp += scores[key];
    }
    float inv_sum = 1.0f / sum_exp;
    for (int key = 0; key < N; key++) {
        scores[key] *= inv_sum;
    }
    
    float out_local[64];
    for (int dd = 0; dd < d; dd++) out_local[dd] = 0.0f;
    
    for (int key = 0; key < N; key++) {
        float s = scores[key];
        for (int dd = 0; dd < d; dd++) {
            out_local[dd] += s * V_shared[key * d + dd];
        }
    }
    
    for (int dd = 0; dd < d; dd++) {
        int out_idx = ((b * N + i) * N + query) * D + head * d + dd;
        scratch[out_idx] = out_local[dd];
    }
}

__global__ void finalize_kernel(
    const float* __restrict__ scratch,
    const float* __restrict__ gate,
    const float* __restrict__ W_out,
    const float* __restrict__ b_out,
    float* __restrict__ output,
    int B, int N, int D
) {
    int pos = blockIdx.x;
    int tid = threadIdx.x;
    
    extern __shared__ float s3[];
    float* gated_shared = s3;
    
    if (tid < D) {
        gated_shared[tid] = scratch[pos * D + tid] * gate[pos * D + tid];
    }
    __syncthreads();
    
    for (int c = tid; c < D; c += blockDim.x) {
        float out_val = b_out[c];
        for (int d = 0; d < D; d++) {
            out_val += W_out[c * D + d] * gated_shared[d];
        }
        output[pos * D + c] = out_val;
    }
}

void launch_preprocess(
    torch::Tensor pair_repr, torch::Tensor ln_weight, torch::Tensor ln_bias,
    torch::Tensor W_query, torch::Tensor W_key, torch::Tensor W_value,
    torch::Tensor W_gate, torch::Tensor b_gate, torch::Tensor W_bias,
    torch::Tensor q, torch::Tensor k, torch::Tensor v,
    torch::Tensor gate, torch::Tensor bias,
    int B, int N, int D, int h, int d
) {
    int total_pos = B * N * N;
    int smem = 256 * sizeof(float);
    preprocess_kernel<<<total_pos, 64, smem>>>(
        pair_repr.data_ptr<float>(), ln_weight.data_ptr<float>(), ln_bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        W_query.data_ptr<float>(), W_key.data_ptr<float>(), W_value.data_ptr<float>(),
        W_gate.data_ptr<float>(), b_gate.data_ptr<float>(), W_bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        q.data_ptr<float>(), k.data_ptr<float>(), v.data_ptr<float>(),
        gate.data_ptr<float>(), bias.data_ptr<float>(),
        B, N, D, h, d
    );
}

void launch_attention(
    torch::Tensor q, torch::Tensor k, torch::Tensor v,
    torch::Tensor bias, torch::Tensor pair_mask,
    torch::Tensor scratch,
    int B, int N, int D, int h, int d
) {
    int blocks = B * N * h;
    int threads = N;
    int smem = 2 * N * d * sizeof(float);
    attention_kernel<<<blocks, threads, smem>>>(
        q.data_ptr<float>(), k.data_ptr<float>(), v.data_ptr<float>(),
        bias.data_ptr<float>(), pair_mask.data_ptr<float>(),
        scratch.data_ptr<float>(),
        B, N, D, h, d
    );
}

void launch_finalize(
    torch::Tensor scratch, torch::Tensor gate,
    torch::Tensor W_out, torch::Tensor b_out,
    torch::Tensor output,
    int B, int N, int D
) {
    int blocks = B * N * N;
    int threads = 64;
    int smem = 128 * sizeof(float);
    finalize_kernel<<<blocks, threads, smem>>>(
        scratch.data_ptr<float>(), gate.data_ptr<float>(),
        W_out.data_ptr<float>(), b_out.data_ptr<float>(),
        output.data_ptr<float>(),
        B, N, D
    );
}
"""

CPP_SOURCE = r"""
void launch_preprocess(
    torch::Tensor pair_repr, torch::Tensor ln_weight, torch::Tensor ln_bias,
    torch::Tensor W_query, torch::Tensor W_key, torch::Tensor W_value,
    torch::Tensor W_gate, torch::Tensor b_gate, torch::Tensor W_bias,
    torch::Tensor q, torch::Tensor k, torch::Tensor v,
    torch::Tensor gate, torch::Tensor bias,
    int B, int N, int D, int h, int d);

void launch_attention(
    torch::Tensor q, torch::Tensor k, torch::Tensor v,
    torch::Tensor bias, torch::Tensor pair_mask,
    torch::Tensor scratch,
    int B, int N, int D, int h, int d);

void launch_finalize(
    torch::Tensor scratch, torch::Tensor gate,
    torch::Tensor W_out, torch::Tensor b_out,
    torch::Tensor output,
    int B, int N, int D);
"""

class ModelNew(nn.Module):
    def __init__(self, pair_dim, num_heads, dropout=0.0):
        super().__init__()
        self.num_heads = num_heads
        self.head_dim = pair_dim // num_heads
        
        self.layer_norm = nn.LayerNorm(pair_dim)
        self.query = nn.Linear(pair_dim, pair_dim, bias=False)
        self.key = nn.Linear(pair_dim, pair_dim, bias=False)
        self.value = nn.Linear(pair_dim, pair_dim, bias=False)
        self.gate = nn.Linear(pair_dim, pair_dim)
        self.bias_proj = nn.Linear(pair_dim, num_heads, bias=False)
        self.out_proj = nn.Linear(pair_dim, pair_dim)
        self.dropout = nn.Dropout(dropout)
        
        self.cuda_module = load_inline(
            name="evoformer_cuda_v3",
            cpp_sources=CPP_SOURCE,
            cuda_sources=CUDA_SOURCE,
            functions=["launch_preprocess", "launch_attention", "launch_finalize"],
            extra_cuda_cflags=["-O3", "--use_fast_math"],
            verbose=False,
        )
        
    def forward(self, pair_repr, pair_mask):
        B, N, _, D = pair_repr.shape
        h = self.num_heads
        d = self.head_dim
        
        pair_repr = pair_repr.contiguous()
        pair_mask = pair_mask.contiguous()
        
        device = pair_repr.device
        
        q = torch.empty(B * N, h, N, d, device=device, dtype=torch.float32)
        k = torch.empty(B * N, h, N, d, device=device, dtype=torch.float32)
        v = torch.empty(B * N, h, N, d, device=device, dtype=torch.float32)
        gate = torch.empty(B, N, N, D, device=device, dtype=torch.float32)
        bias = torch.empty(B, h, N, N, device=device, dtype=torch.float32)
        scratch = torch.empty(B, N, N, D, device=device, dtype=torch.float32)
        output = torch.empty(B, N, N, D, device=device, dtype=torch.float32)
        
        self.cuda_module.launch_preprocess(
            pair_repr,
            self.layer_norm.weight,
            self.layer_norm.bias,
            self.query.weight,
            self.key.weight,
            self.value.weight,
            self.gate.weight,
            self.gate.bias,
            self.bias_proj.weight,
            q, k, v, gate, bias,
            B, N, D, h, d
        )
        
        self.cuda_module.launch_attention(
            q, k, v, bias, pair_mask,
            scratch,
            B, N, D, h, d
        )
        
        self.cuda_module.launch_finalize(
            scratch, gate,
            self.out_proj.weight,
            self.out_proj.bias,
            output,
            B, N, D
        )
        
        return output
